How to Roll

Roll a d10 and a d100, minus 1 from the d10.

The d10 is the 100s place and the d100 is the tens and ones.

E.g. if you roll a 10 (-1) and a 56 that's 396.

If you roll a 1 (-1) and a 04 that's 4.

1 (-1) and a 00 becomes 1000.

Loot Chart

#1

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Rare
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Gray
- Passive: Instant Hack
    - Twice a run you can add 15 to a Hacking check. Each time you finish a Hack successfully gain 500 Essenceand a random piece of gear.
- Essence Value: 2000
- Credit Value: 200
- Aesthetic: Cortez (Western)

#2

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Rare
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Neutral
- Passive: Battery
    - Can store up to 7 Energy for use later.
- Essence Value: 2000
- Credit Value: 200
- Aesthetic: Rtolkan (Steampunk)

#3

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Rare
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Red
- Passive: Pain Rage
    - Spend HP to get a Damage Plus on one attack equal to the HP spent x1.5. (Can only be done once per turn.)
- Essence Value: 2000
- Credit Value: 200
- Aesthetic: Jiyyagan (Survivor/Jungle)

#4

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Rare
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Neutral
- Passive: Extra Gear Slots
    - Gain 3 extra Gear Slots of your choice.
- Essence Value: 2000
- Credit Value: 200
- Aesthetic: Cortez (Western)

#5

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Rare
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Green
- Passive: Wild Growth
    - Whenever you gain HP in combat you may deal 1 damage to any target for every 1 HP you heal.
    - Whenever anybody else in your party gains HP in combat you may deal 1 damage to any target for every 3 HP they heal.
- Essence Value: 2000
- Credit Value: 200
- Aesthetic: Pbosh (Viking/Heavy, Rough Metal)

#6

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Rare
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Blue
- Passive: Environmental Damage
    - When you cause a target to fall, you can make the target take a d12 of damage per tile it falls. You may deal a d10 of damage per tile a target travels when you push or pull them against a wall or hard surface.
- Essence Value: 2000
- Credit Value: 200
- Aesthetic: Asticarian (Modern)

- Gear: Kernel
